### [153] [98$\times$ Faster LLM Routing Without a Dedicated GPU: Flash Attention, Prompt Compression, and Near-Streaming for the vLLM Semantic Router](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12646)
*Xunzhuo Liu,Bowei He,Xue Liu,Andy Luo,Haichen Zhang,Huamin Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种用于 LLM 的 vLLM 语义路由器，通过分阶段优化解决了路由器的延迟和内存瓶颈问题，实现了 98 倍的性能提升，并将 GPU 占用空间减至 800MB 以下，从而能够与 LLM 推理共享 GPU。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的系统级路由器在处理 LLM 请求时需要快速且资源占用低，但标准的注意力机制在长上下文下内存消耗过大 ($O(n^2)$)，无法满足需求，并且需要避免占用昂贵的 GPU 资源。

Method: 研究提出了三阶段优化：1. 使用自定义 CK Flash Attention 算子将注意力内存从 $O(n^2)$ 降至 $O(n)$；2. 采用 TextRank、位置加权、TF-IDF 和新颖性评分等 NLP 提示压缩技术，将输入限制在约 512 个 token；3. 引入近流式分块处理和零拷贝 JSON，消除序列化开销。

Result: 通过三阶段优化，端到端延迟从 4918ms 降低到 50ms（98 倍提升），16K token 的路由时间缩短至 108ms，路由器 GPU 占用空间小于 800MB。

Conclusion: 优化的 vLLM 语义路由器能够高效处理长上下文 LLM 请求，具有低延迟和低内存占用的特点，可以与 LLM 推理共享 GPU，无需专用加速器。

Abstract: System-level routers that intercept LLM requests for safety classification, domain routing, and PII detection must be both fast and operationally lightweight: they should add minimal latency to every request, yet not require a dedicated GPU -- an expensive resource better used for LLM inference itself. When the router co-locates on the same GPU as vLLM serving instances, standard attention's $O(n^2)$ memory makes long-context classification (8K--32K tokens) impossible: at 8K tokens, three concurrent classifiers need ${\sim}$4.5\,GB for attention masks alone, far exceeding the memory left by vLLM. We present three staged optimizations for the vLLM Semantic Router, benchmarked on AMD Instinct MI300X, that solve both the latency and the memory problem. \emph{Stage~1}: a custom CK Flash Attention operator for ONNX Runtime on ROCm reduces attention memory from $O(n^2)$ to $O(n)$ and end-to-end (E2E) latency from 4{,}918\,ms to 127\,ms (\textbf{38.7$\times$}), enabling 8K--32K tokens where SDPA OOMs. \emph{Stage~2}: classical NLP prompt compression (TextRank, position weighting, TF-IDF, and novelty scoring) reduces all inputs to ${\sim}$512 tokens without neural inference, capping both latency and GPU memory at a constant regardless of original prompt length (E2E 127$\to$62\,ms, \textbf{2.0$\times$}). \emph{Stage~3}: near-streaming body processing with adaptive chunking and zero-copy JSON eliminates serialization overhead (E2E 62$\to$50\,ms, \textbf{1.2$\times$}). Cumulatively: \textbf{98$\times$} improvement (4{,}918\,ms to 50\,ms), 16K-token routing in 108\,ms, and a total router GPU footprint under 800\,MB -- small enough to share a GPU with LLM serving and removing the need for a dedicated accelerator. Stage~1 targets AMD ROCm (NVIDIA GPUs already have FlashAttention via cuDNN); Stages~2 and~3 are hardware-agnostic.

</details>


### [154] [Experimental evidence of progressive ChatGPT models self-convergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12683)
*Konstantinos F. Xylogiannopoulos,Petros Xanthopoulos,Panagiotis Karampelas,Georgios A. Bakamitsos*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 近期发布的ChatGPT模型在递归训练下，其输出文本的多样性有所下降，这可能与训练数据中合成数据的增加有关，作者称之为“模型自收敛”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究未能从纵向角度评估LLM在递归训练下面临的模型崩溃问题，即合成数据导致输出质量下降的长期影响。

Method: 使用文本相似度指标，在温度参数设置为1的情况下，评估不同ChatGPT版本生成文本的多样性。

Result: 发现近期发布的ChatGPT模型生成文本的多样性有可衡量的下降，即使在明确要求多样性的情况下也是如此。

Conclusion: 近期ChatGPT版本的输出多样性下降，可能归因于其训练数据中合成数据的增加。这种现象被称为“模型自收敛”，表现为不同ChatGPT版本之间生成文本的相似度逐渐增加。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) that undergo recursive training on synthetically generated data are susceptible to model collapse, a phenomenon marked by the generation of meaningless output. Existing research has examined this issue from either theoretical or empirical perspectives, often focusing on a single model trained recursively on its own outputs. While prior studies have cautioned against the potential degradation of LLM output quality under such conditions, no longitudinal investigation has yet been conducted to assess this effect over time. In this study, we employ a text similarity metric to evaluate different ChatGPT models' capacity to generate diverse textual outputs. Our findings indicate a measurable decline of recent ChatGPT releases' ability to produce varied text, even when explicitly prompted to do so, by setting the temperature parameter to one. The observed reduction in output diversity may be attributed to the influence of the amounts of synthetic data incorporated within their training datasets as the result of internet infiltration by LLM generated data. The phenomenon is defined as model self-convergence because of the gradual increase of similarities of produced texts among different ChatGPT versions.

### [155] [MetaKE: Meta-learning Aligned Knowledge Editing via Bi-level Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12677)
*Shuxin Liu,Ou Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为 MetaKE 的新知识编辑框架，通过双层优化将编辑目标重塑为可学习的元参数，并引入结构化梯度代理来解决语义执行不匹配问题，从而提高知识编辑的准确性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识编辑方法存在“语义-执行断裂”问题，即编辑目标与模型可编辑区域不匹配，导致梯度截断和编辑失败。

Method: 将知识编辑重构为双层优化问题。上层优化器学习可行的编辑目标以最大化编辑后性能，下层求解器执行编辑。通过推导“结构化梯度代理”将可编辑性约束反向传播到目标学习阶段。

Result: MetaKE 在理论上证明了其能将编辑方向与模型的可行流形对齐。实验表明，MetaKE 显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: MetaKE 提供了一种新的知识编辑视角，通过双层优化和结构化梯度代理有效解决了语义-执行断裂问题，显著提升了知识编辑的效果。

Abstract: Knowledge editing (KE) aims to precisely rectify specific knowledge in Large Language Models (LLMs) without disrupting general capabilities. State-of-the-art methods suffer from an open-loop control mismatch. We identify a critical "Semantic-Execution Disconnect": the semantic target is derived independently without feedback from the downstream's feasible region. This misalignment often causes valid semantic targets to fall within the prohibited space, resulting in gradient truncation and editing failure. To bridge this gap, we propose MetaKE (Meta-learning Aligned Knowledge Editing), a new framework that reframes KE as a bi-level optimization problem. Departing from static calculation, MetaKE treats the edit target as a learnable meta-parameter: the upper-level optimizer seeks a feasible target to maximize post-edit performance, while the lower-level solver executes the editing. To address the challenge of differentiating through complex solvers, we derive a Structural Gradient Proxy, which explicitly backpropagates editability constraints to the target learning phase. Theoretical analysis demonstrates that MetaKE automatically aligns the edit direction with the model's feasible manifold. Extensive experiments confirm that MetaKE significantly outperforms strong baselines, offering a new perspective on knowledge editing.

</details>

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) is a promising approach for improving code generation in large language models, but its effectiveness is limited by weak and static verification signals in existing coding RL datasets. In this paper, we propose a solution-conditioned and adversarial verification framework that iteratively refines test cases based on the execution behaviors of candidate solutions, with the goal of increasing difficulty, improving discriminative power, and reducing redundancy. Based on this framework, we introduce EvolveCoder-22k, a large-scale coding reinforcement learning dataset constructed through multiple rounds of adversarial test case evolution. Empirical analysis shows that iterative refinement substantially strengthens verification, with pass@1 decreasing from 43.80 to 31.22. Reinforcement learning on EvolveCoder-22k yields stable optimization and consistent performance gains, improving Qwen3-4B by an average of 4.2 points across four downstream benchmarks and outperforming strong 4B-scale baselines. Our results highlight the importance of adversarial, solution-conditioned verification for effective and scalable reinforcement learning in code generation.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 LLMs 成为宗教知识的重要来源，研究其对不同宗教群体（特别是伊斯兰教逊尼派和什叶派）是否公平至关重要。

Method: 开发了一个名为 SectEval 的测试集（包含 88 个问题），并将其翻译成英文和印地文。使用该测试集评估了 15 个主流 LLM 模型（包括专有和开源模型）在处理逊尼派和什叶派问题时的偏见。

Result: 研究发现 LLMs 的偏见因语言而异。在英文中，许多模型（如 DeepSeek-v3 和 GPT-4o）倾向于什叶派答案，而在印地文中，这些模型则倾向于逊尼派答案。先进的模型（如 Claude-3.5）会根据用户地理位置调整答案，而较小的模型（尤其是在印地文中）则倾向于坚持逊尼派观点。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) becomes a popular source for religious knowledge, it is important to know if it treats different groups fairly. This study is the first to measure how LLMs handle the differences between the two main sects of Islam: Sunni and Shia. We present a test called SectEval, available in both English and Hindi, consisting of 88 questions, to check the bias-ness of 15 top LLM models, both proprietary and open-weights. Our results show a major inconsistency based on language. In English, many powerful models DeepSeek-v3 and GPT-4o often favored Shia answers. However, when asked the exact same questions in Hindi, these models switched to favoring Sunni answers. This means a user could get completely different religious advice just by changing languages. We also looked at how models react to location. Advanced models Claude-3.5 changed their answers to match the user's country-giving Shia answers to a user from Iran and Sunni answers to a user from Saudi Arabia. In contrast, smaller models (especially in Hindi) ignored the user's location and stuck to a Sunni viewpoint. These findings show that AI is not neutral; its religious ``truth'' changes depending on the language you speak and the country you claim to be from. The data set is available at https://github.com/secteval/SectEval/

### [159] [SteerRM: Debiasing Reward Models via Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12795)
*Mengyuan Sun,Zhuohao Yu,Weizheng Gu,Shikun Zhang,Wei Ye*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的奖励模型（RM）偏向于表面风格提示，而不是语义上更优的响应，并且现有的去偏方法需要重新训练或修改架构，直接抑制激活会因表示纠缠而降低性能。

Method: SteerRM采用训练无关的方法，利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）干预。该方法使用对比配对响应隔离风格效应，通过强度-稳定性标准识别与偏见相关的SAE特征，并在推理时抑制这些特征。

Result: 在RM-Bench的六个奖励模型上，SteerRM平均提高了Hard-split准确率7.3个百分点，同时保持了整体性能。在Gemma奖励模型和受控非格式偏见上的结果表明，该方法可以推广到不同的RM架构和偏见类型。研究还发现，格式相关的特征集中在浅层，并且可以在模型之间转移，揭示了共享的架构级别偏见编码模式。

Conclusion: 基于SAE的干预可以缓解奖励模型的偏见，而无需重新训练，为对齐流水线提供了一种实用且可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: Reward models (RMs) are critical components of alignment pipelines, yet they exhibit biases toward superficial stylistic cues, preferring better-presented responses over semantically superior ones. Existing debiasing methods typically require retraining or architectural modifications, while direct activation suppression degrades performance due to representation entanglement. We propose SteerRM, the first training-free method for debiasing reward models using Sparse Autoencoder (SAE)-based interventions. SteerRM isolates stylistic effects using contrastive paired responses, identifies bias-related SAE features with a strength-stability criterion, and suppresses them at inference time. Across six reward models on RM-Bench, SteerRM improves Hard-split accuracy by 7.3 points on average while preserving overall performance. Results on a Gemma-based reward model and a controlled non-format bias further suggest generalization across RM architectures and bias types. We further find that format-related features are concentrated in shallow layers and transfer across models, revealing shared architecture-level bias encoding patterns. These results show that SAE-based interventions can mitigate reward-model biases without retraining, providing a practical and interpretable solution for alignment pipelines.

### [160] [Adaptive Vision-Language Model Routing for Computer Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12823)
*Xunzhuo Liu,Bowei He,Xue Liu,Andy Luo,Haichen Zhang,Huamin Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种自适应视觉语言模型（VLM）路由（AVR）框架，通过根据操作难度动态选择最经济实惠但准确度满足要求的VLM来降低计算机使用代理（CUA）的推理成本，同时保持接近全大模型基线的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的CUA系统将所有操作都交给单一固定VLM处理，但VLM的准确率差异很大，导致成本高且效率低下。需要一种方法来根据操作难度选择合适的VLM，以平衡成本和准确性。

Method: AVR框架在CUA和VLM池之间插入了一个语义路由层。它通过多模态嵌入估计操作难度，利用小型VLM评估置信度，并将操作路由到能满足目标可靠性阈值的最经济VLM。对于有记忆的“温暖”代理，上下文信息可以缩小小型和大型模型之间的能力差距。路由问题被形式化为成本-准确性权衡，并推导出基于阈值的模型选择策略。

Result: 在ScreenSpot-Pro和OpenClaw基准测试中，AVR可以将推理成本降低高达78%，同时准确率仅比使用所有大型模型的基线低2个百分点。AVR与Visual Confused Deputy结合使用时，还能将高风险操作直接转交给最强的模型，实现效率和安全性的统一。

Conclusion: AVR是一种有效的框架，能够通过自适应地选择VLM来显著降低CUA的推理成本，同时保持高准确率，并且能够与安全机制结合，提高系统的整体性能和安全性。

Abstract: Computer Use Agents (CUAs) translate natural-language instructions into Graphical User Interface (GUI) actions such as clicks, keystrokes, and scrolls by relying on a Vision-Language Model (VLM) to interpret screenshots and predict grounded tool calls. However, grounding accuracy varies dramatically across VLMs, while current CUA systems typically route every action to a single fixed model regardless of difficulty. We propose \textbf{Adaptive VLM Routing} (AVR), a framework that inserts a lightweight semantic routing layer between the CUA orchestrator and a pool of VLMs. For each tool call, AVR estimates action difficulty from multimodal embeddings, probes a small VLM to measure confidence, and routes the action to the cheapest model whose predicted accuracy satisfies a target reliability threshold. For \textit{warm} agents with memory of prior UI interactions, retrieved context further narrows the capability gap between small and large models, allowing many actions to be handled without escalation. We formalize routing as a cost--accuracy trade-off, derive a threshold-based policy for model selection, and evaluate AVR using ScreenSpot-Pro grounding data together with the OpenClaw agent routing benchmark. Across these settings, AVR projects inference cost reductions of up to 78\% while staying within 2 percentage points of an all-large-model baseline. When combined with the Visual Confused Deputy guardrail, AVR also escalates high-risk actions directly to the strongest available model, unifying efficiency and safety within a single routing framework. Materials are also provided Model, benchmark, and code: https://github.com/vllm-project/semantic-router.

### [161] [Rethinking Multiple-Choice Questions for RLVR: Unlocking Potential via Distractor Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12826)
*Xu Guo,Qiming Ge,Jian Tong,Kedi Chen,Jin Zhang,Xiaogui Yang,Xuan Gao,Haijun Lv,Zhihui Lu,Yicheng Zou,Qipeng Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为迭代式干扰项策选（IDC）的框架，用于改进基于强化学习的可验证奖励（RLVR）训练。通过主动生成高质量的干扰项，IDC 可以有效阻止模型通过排除法进行猜测，促进深度推理，从而在 RLVR 训练中取得显著的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于多项选择题（MCQ）的 RLVR 方法存在奖励欺骗（reward hacking）的问题，即模型可能通过随机猜测或简单排除法来“绕过”推理过程。而将 MCQ 转换为开放式问题会丢失专家设计的干扰项所提供的对比信号。因此，研究如何设计更好的干扰项以促进 RLVR 训练是必要的。

Method: 作者系统地研究了选项设计对 RLVR 的影响，发现了选项数量不匹配和干扰项强度对性能的影响。在此基础上，提出迭代式干扰项策选（IDC）框架，该框架能够主动构建高质量的干扰项，以阻止排除法快捷方式并促进深度推理。

Result: 实验结果表明，IDC 框架能够有效提升干扰项的质量，并在 RLVR 训练中相比原始数据取得了显著的性能提升。即使在使用两选项问题时，强干扰项也能有效缓解随机猜测，实现有效的 RLVR 训练。

Conclusion: 选项设计，特别是干扰项的质量，对 RLVR 的训练效果至关重要。IDC 框架通过迭代地策选高质量干扰项，能够有效地解决奖励欺骗问题，提升模型的推理能力，为 RLVR 训练提供了一种有效的方法。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) significantly enhances the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models. When applied to RLVR, Multiple-Choice Questions (MCQs) offer a scalable source of verifiable data but risk inducing reward hacking, where models shortcut reasoning via random guessing or simple elimination. Current approaches often mitigate this by converting MCQs to open-ended formats, thereby discarding the contrastive signal provided by expert-designed distractors. In this work, we systematically investigate the impact of option design on RLVR. Our analysis highlights two primary insights: (1) Mismatches in option counts between training and testing degrade performance. (2) Strong distractors effectively mitigate random guessing, enabling effective RLVR training even with 2-way questions. Motivated by these findings, we propose Iterative Distractor Curation (IDC), a framework that actively constructs high-quality distractors to block elimination shortcuts and promote deep reasoning. Experiments on various benchmarks demonstrate that our method effectively enhances distractor quality and yields significant gains in RLVR training compared to the original data.

Method: 研究者将BabyBERTa扩展到英法双语场景，对比了两种训练语料：儿童指导语（约2.5M tokens）和多领域语料（约10M tokens）。同时，引入了新的评估资源，包括法语版的QAMR和QASRL，以及英法多领域语料。对模型进行了句法和语义任务的评估，并与仅在Wikipedia上训练的模型进行了比较。

Result: 在单语设置下，儿童指导语有利于语法判断，而Wikipedia语料则持续有利于语义任务。双语预训练在文本蕴含任务上带来了显著的提升，特别是对法语。这些模式在BabyBERTa、RoBERTa和LTG-BERT等不同模型架构上都出现了相似的趋势。

Conclusion: 训练语料的类型对紧凑型语言模型在不同任务上的表现有着情境依赖性的影响。儿童指导语在单语语法判断上表现突出，而多领域语料（包括Wikipedia）在语义任务上更有优势。双语预训练能够有效提升文本蕴含能力，尤其是对于模型处理的非英语语言（在此研究中为法语）。研究结果表明，这些趋势在不同的语言模型架构中是普遍存在的。

Abstract: Research on developmentally plausible language models has largely focused on English, leaving open questions about multilingual settings. We present a systematic study of compact language models by extending BabyBERTa to English-French scenarios under strictly size-matched data conditions, covering monolingual, bilingual, and cross-lingual settings. Our design contrasts two types of training corpora: (i) child-directed speech (about 2.5M tokens), following BabyBERTa and related work, and (ii) multi-domain corpora (about 10M tokens), extending the BabyLM framework to French. To enable fair evaluation, we also introduce new resources, including French versions of QAMR and QASRL, as well as English and French multi-domain corpora.
  We evaluate the models on both syntactic and semantic tasks and compare them with models trained on Wikipedia-only data. The results reveal context-dependent effects: training on Wikipedia consistently benefits semantic tasks, whereas child-directed speech improves grammatical judgments in monolingual settings. Bilingual pretraining yields notable gains for textual entailment, with particularly strong improvements for French. Importantly, similar patterns emerge across BabyBERTa, RoBERTa, and LTG-BERT, suggesting consistent trends across architectures.

Method: DS$^2$-Instruct 框架是一个零样本方法。首先，它生成任务信息关键词以确保领域覆盖全面；然后，将这些关键词与布鲁姆分类法中的不同认知层次配对，创建多样化的指令；最后，利用自洽性验证来保证数据质量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的SSD方法在PCA降维时缺乏系统性的组件数量选择标准，导致分析结果存在不确定性。

Method: 提出了一种PCA扫描程序（PCA sweep procedure），通过联合优化表示能力、梯度可解释性和稳定性来选择最优的PCA组件数量（K）。

Result: 在AI语料研究中，新的方法成功识别出与“赞赏”（Admiration）自恋特质相关的语义梯度，该梯度区分了对AI持乐观、合作态度的言论与不信任、嘲讽言论。而与“竞争”（Rivalry）特质相关的梯度则未出现稳健的关联。对比发现，使用启发式方法选择高维度的PCA结果会产生模糊、结构松散的聚类。

Conclusion: PCA扫描程序能够约束SSD分析中的研究者自由度，同时保持其解释性目标，从而支持透明且有心理学意义的内涵意义分析。此方法有望改进SSD在心理学研究中的应用。

Abstract: Supervised Semantic Differential (SSD) is a mixed quantitative-interpretive method that models how text meaning varies with continuous individual-difference variables by estimating a semantic gradient in an embedding space and interpreting its poles through clustering and text retrieval. SSD applies PCA before regression, but currently no systematic method exists for choosing the number of retained components, introducing avoidable researcher degrees of freedom in the analysis pipeline. We propose a PCA sweep procedure that treats dimensionality selection as a joint criterion over representation capacity, gradient interpretability, and stability across nearby values of K. We illustrate the method on a corpus of short posts about artificial intelligence written by Prolific participants who also completed Admiration and Rivalry narcissism scales. The sweep yields a stable, interpretable Admiration-related gradient contrasting optimistic, collaborative framings of AI with distrustful and derisive discourse, while no robust alignment emerges for Rivalry. We also show that a counterfactual using a high-PCA dimension solution heuristic produces diffuse, weakly structured clusters instead, reinforcing the value of the sweep-based choice of K. The case study shows how the PCA sweep constrains researcher degrees of freedom while preserving SSD's interpretive aims, supporting transparent and psychologically meaningful analyses of connotative meaning.

### [170] [Neuron-Aware Data Selection In Instruction Tuning For Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13201)
*Xin Chen,Junchao Wu,Shu Yang,Runzhe Zhan,Zeyu Wu,Min Yang,Shujian Huang,Lidia S. Chao,Derek F. Wong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为NAIT的新框架，通过分析神经元激活模式的相似性来从指令调优（IT）数据集中选择最优子集，以提升大型语言模型（LLMs）的能力。实验表明，NAIT选择的10%数据子集在多项任务上优于其他方法，并且发现具有逻辑推理和编程特性的IT数据具有更强的通用迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过度的指令调优（IT）数据会损害LLMs的性能，而精心选择高质量的IT数据子集则能显著提升其能力。因此，如何从IT数据集中识别出最有效的数据子集来发展LLMs的特定或通用能力成为了一个关键挑战。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为NAIT的框架，它通过分析IT数据集与目标领域能力之间神经元激活模式的相似性来评估IT数据的影响。NAIT从目标领域能力的域内数据集中捕获神经元激活模式，构建可重用和可迁移的神经元激活特征。然后，它基于候选样本与目标能力预期激活特征之间的相似性来评估和选择最优样本。

Result: 实验结果表明，使用NAIT选择的10% Alpaca-GPT4 IT数据子集进行训练，在各种任务上的表现始终优于依赖外部高级模型或基于不确定性特征的方法。研究还揭示了神经元激活特征在LLMs不同能力之间的迁移性。特别是，具有更多逻辑推理和编程特性的IT数据具有很强的通用迁移性，而一个稳定的核心数据子集足以持续激活模型的基本能力并普遍提升性能。

Conclusion: NAIT框架能够有效地从指令调优数据集中选择出对提升LLMs性能至关重要的数据子集。研究发现，IT数据的逻辑推理和编程特性使其具备强大的通用迁移能力，而稳定的核心数据子集则能普遍提升模型性能。

Abstract: Instruction Tuning (IT) has been proven to be an effective approach to unlock the powerful capabilities of large language models (LLMs). Recent studies indicate that excessive IT data can degrade LLMs performance, while carefully selecting a small subset of high-quality IT data can significantly enhance their capabilities. Therefore, identifying the most efficient subset data from the IT dataset to effectively develop either specific or general abilities in LLMs has become a critical challenge. To address this, we propose a novel and efficient framework called NAIT. NAIT evaluates the impact of IT data on LLMs performance by analyzing the similarity of neuron activation patterns between the IT dataset and the target domain capability. Specifically, NAIT captures neuron activation patterns from in-domain datasets of target domain capabilities to construct reusable and transferable neuron activation features. It then evaluates and selects optimal samples based on the similarity between candidate samples and the expected activation features of the target capabilities. Experimental results show that training on the 10\% Alpaca-GPT4 IT data subset selected by NAIT consistently outperforms methods that rely on external advanced models or uncertainty-based features across various tasks. Our findings also reveal the transferability of neuron activation features across different capabilities of LLMs. In particular, IT data with more logical reasoning and programmatic features possesses strong general transferability, enabling models to develop stronger capabilities across multiple tasks, while a stable core subset of data is sufficient to consistently activate fundamental model capabilities and universally improve performance across diverse tasks.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型在低资源语言的机器翻译方面表现不佳，而现有的后训练方法需要高质量的平行语料，这在低资源语言中往往难以获得。本研究旨在克服这一挑战，仅利用单语文本来提高LLMs在低资源语言上的翻译能力。

Method: WALAR是一种强化学习（RL）训练方法，利用单语文本进行训练。该方法通过缓解现有源语言多语言质量评估（QE）模型中的“漏洞”（holes）来优化RL训练的奖励。具体技术包括词对齐和语言对齐。研究人员使用WALAR对一个支持101种语言的LLM进行了持续训练。

Result: 经过WALAR训练的模型在Flores-101数据集的1400个语言方向上，显著优于最强的开源多语言LLM之一LLaMAX。

Conclusion: WALAR是一种有效的利用单语文本提升LLMs在低资源语言翻译能力的方法，通过解决QE模型中的漏洞，能够显著提高多语言LLMs的翻译性能，并且在实际应用中取得了优于现有 SOTA 模型的成果。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capability in machine translation on high-resource language pairs, yet their performance on low-resource translation still lags behind. Existing post-training methods rely heavily on high-quality parallel data, which are often scarce or unavailable for low-resource languages. In this paper, we introduce WALAR, a reinforcement training method using only monolingual text to elevate LLMs' translation capabilities on massive low-resource languages while retaining their performance on high-resource languages. Our key insight is based on the observation of failure modes (or "holes") in existing source-based multilingual quality estimation (QE) models. Reinforcement learning (RL) using these QE models tends to amplify such holes, resulting in poorer multilingual LLMs. We develop techniques including word alignment and language alignment to mitigate such holes in WALAR's reward for RL training. We continually trained an LLM supporting translation of 101 languages using WALAR. The experiments show that our new model outperforms LLaMAX, one of the strongest open-source multilingual LLMs by a large margin on 1400 language directions on Flores-101 dataset.

</details>

### [172] [GNN-DIP: Neural Corridor Selection for Decomposition-Based Motion Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12361)
*Peng Xie,Yanlinag Huang,Wenyuan Wu,Amr Alanwar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 GNN-DIP 的新框架，通过图神经网络（GNN）与分解知情规划器（DIP）结合，解决了机器人运动规划中的狭窄通道问题，显著提高了规划效率和成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于采样的方法在规划狭窄通道时效率低下，而基于分解的方法虽然能解决样本稀疏和碰撞检查问题，但在走廊选择方面存在组合爆炸的瓶颈。因此，需要一种更有效的方法来处理这类场景。

Method: 该框架使用图神经网络（GNN）预测单元邻接图上的“门户得分”，从而引导走廊搜索。结合二维中的约束 Delaunay 三角剖分（CDT）和漏斗算法，以及三维中的平板凸分解和门户面采样，实现了路径规划。

Result: 在二维狭窄通道、三维瓶颈环境和动态二维场景的基准测试中，GNN-DIP 实现了 99%-100% 的成功率，并且规划速度比基于采样的方法快 2-280 倍。

Conclusion: GNN-DIP 框架能够有效地解决机器人运动规划中的狭窄通道问题，通过 GNN 引导走廊搜索，显著提高了规划的效率和鲁棒性，并在各种复杂场景下表现出色。

Abstract: Motion planning through narrow passages remains a core challenge: sampling-based planners rarely place samples inside these narrow but critical regions, and even when samples land inside a passage, the straight-line connections between them run close to obstacle boundaries and are frequently rejected by collision checking. Decomposition-based planners resolve both issues by partitioning free space into convex cells -- every passage is captured exactly as a cell boundary, and any path within a cell is collision-free by construction. However, the number of candidate corridors through the cell graph grows combinatorially with environment complexity, creating a bottleneck in corridor selection. We present GNN-DIP, a framework that addresses this by integrating a Graph Neural Network (GNN) with a two-phase Decomposition-Informed Planner (DIP). The GNN predicts portal scores on the cell adjacency graph to bias corridor search toward near-optimal regions while preserving completeness. In 2D, Constrained Delaunay Triangulation (CDT) with the Funnel algorithm yields exact shortest paths within corridors; in 3D, Slab convex decomposition with portal-face sampling provides near-optimal path evaluation. Benchmarks on 2D narrow-passage scenarios, 3D bottleneck environments with up to 246 obstacles, and dynamic 2D settings show that GNN-DIP achieves 99--100% success rates with 2--280 times speedup over sampling-based baselines.

</details>


### [173] [A Learning-Based Approach for Contact Detection, Localization, and Force Estimation of Continuum Manipulators With Integrated OFDR Optical Fiber](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12347)
*Mobina Tavangarifard,Jonathan S. Kacines,Qiyu Li,Farshid Alambeigi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于级联学习的框架（CLF），利用嵌入在连续操纵器（CM）一侧的单根分布式光频域反射（OFDR）光纤，实现了接触检测、位置和力大小的联合估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在微创手术中，连续操纵器（CM）因其柔顺性和在狭窄解剖环境中的导航能力而被广泛应用。然而，其分布式形变给力感知、接触检测、定位和力估计带来了挑战，特别是在未知弧长位置发生交互时。因此，需要一种能够应对这些挑战的感知方法。

Method: 该研究提出了一种级联学习框架（CLF）。该框架使用一根嵌入在CM一侧的分布式OFDR光纤，收集沿着机械臂骨干的密集应变测量数据。首先，利用梯度提升分类器检测接触。然后，利用CNN--FiLM模型结合OFDR数据来估计接触位置和交互力的大小，该模型能预测机械臂沿空间的力分布。

Result: 通过在传感器化腱驱动CM和受阻环境中进行实验验证，结果表明，单根分布式OFDR光纤能够提供足够的信息，联合推断出连续操纵器中的接触发生、位置和力。

Conclusion: 所提出的级联学习框架（CLF）结合分布式OFDR光纤，能够有效地解决连续操纵器在未知位置的接触检测和力估计问题，为CM在复杂环境下的安全操作提供了技术支持。

Abstract: Continuum manipulators (CMs) are widely used in minimally invasive procedures due to their compliant structure and ability to navigate deep and confined anatomical environments. However, their distributed deformation makes force sensing, contact detection, localization, and force estimation challenging, particularly when interactions occur at unknown arc-length locations along the robot. To address this problem, we propose a cascade learning-based framework (CLF) for CMs instrumented with a single distributed Optical Frequency Domain Reflectometry (OFDR) fiber embedded along one side of the robot. The OFDR sensor provides dense strain measurements along the manipulator backbone, capturing strain perturbations caused by external interactions. The proposed CLF first detects contact using a Gradient Boosting classifier and then estimates contact location and interaction force magnitude using a CNN--FiLM model that predicts a spatial force distribution along the manipulator. Experimental validation on a sensorized tendon-driven CM in an obstructed environment demonstrates that a single distributed OFDR fiber provides sufficient information to jointly infer contact occurrence, location, and force in continuum manipulators.

### [174] [Push, Press, Slide: Mode-Aware Planar Contact Manipulation via Reduced-Order Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12399)
*Melih Özcan,Ozgur S. Oguz,Umut Orguner*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种基于接触拓扑选择和降阶运动学模型的非抓取式平面操作框架，通过将复杂的力-扭矩限制曲面力学抽象为离散模型库，简化了控制计算，实现了快速、无需优化的操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的非抓取式平面操作（如推、压滑）由于其复杂的力学特性，通常需要计算量大的迭代控制方法。本研究旨在克服这一挑战，提出一种更高效的控制框架。

Method: 该框架基于接触拓扑选择和降阶运动学建模。通过将复杂的力-扭矩限制曲面力学抽象为离散的物理模型库，并将不同的单臂和双臂接触拓扑映射到简单的非完整动力学模型（例如，用于压滑运动的简化版独轮车模型）。通过将轨迹生成锚定在这些降阶模型上，计算所需物体力矩，并通过直接代数分配器分配可行、受限于摩擦力的接触力。同时，考虑了机械臂运动学以确保长时域的可行性。

Result: 该框架计算速度快，无需优化。在模拟中，其在多种单臂和双臂操作任务中均表现良好。

Conclusion: 提出的模式感知框架通过抽象复杂的接触力学为离散模型，有效简化了非抓取式平面操作的控制，实现了高效、无需优化的计算，并在仿真中证明了其有效性。

Abstract: Non-prehensile planar manipulation, including pushing and press-and-slide, is critical for diverse robotic tasks, but notoriously challenging due to hybrid contact mechanics, under-actuation, and asymmetric friction limits that traditionally necessitate computationally expensive iterative control. In this paper, we propose a mode-aware framework for planar manipulation with one or two robotic arms based on contact topology selection and reduced-order kinematic modeling. Our core insight is that complex wrench-twist limit surface mechanics can be abstracted into a discrete library of physically intuitive models. We systematically map various single-arm and bimanual contact topologies to simple non-holonomic formulations, e.g. unicycle for simplified press-and-slide motion. By anchoring trajectory generation to these reduced-order models, our framework computes the required object wrench and distributes feasible, friction-bounded contact forces via a direct algebraic allocator. We incorporate manipulator kinematics to ensure long-horizon feasibility and demonstrate our fast, optimization-free approach in simulation across diverse single-arm and bimanual manipulation tasks.

</details>


### [175] [Beyond Motion Imitation: Is Human Motion Data Alone Sufficient to Explain Gait Control and Biomechanics?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12408)
*Xinyi Liu,Jangwhan Ahn,Edgar Lobaton,Jennie Si,He Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 将足地交互（如接触力和质心）纳入强化学习中的运动模仿奖励项，可以显著提高步态动力学的预测精度，纠正仅模仿运动学可能导致的生物力学不一致问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日益增长的运动模仿学习（IL）在人体生物力学和可穿戴机器人领域的兴趣，促使研究者探索如何通过改进IL框架来更准确地估计步态的运动学和动力学。

Method: 研究者在一个基于强化学习的IL框架中，探索了将额外的足地交互测量（如接触力和质心）作为奖励项，如何影响人体步态运动学和动力学的估计。

Result: 研究发现，仅准确复现前进运动学不足以保证生物力学上合理的关节动力学。将足地接触和接触力加入IL奖励项，能够预测前向行走模拟中的关节力矩，且这些力矩与逆动力学计算结果显著更接近。

Conclusion: 仅依赖运动学的IL方法可能优先考虑运动学匹配而牺牲物理一致性。在人体生物力学和可穿戴机器人共设计等领域应用IL时，需要引入基于动力学的奖励塑造（如地面反作用力和质心信息），以获得物理上一致的步态表示。

Abstract: With the growing interest in motion imitation learning (IL) for human biomechanics and wearable robotics, this study investigates how additional foot-ground interaction measures, used as reward terms, affect human gait kinematics and kinetics estimation within a reinforcement learning-based IL framework. Results indicate that accurate reproduction of forward kinematics alone does not ensure biomechanically plausible joint kinetics. Adding foot-ground contacts and contact forces to the IL reward terms enables the prediction of joint moments in forward walking simulation, which are significantly closer to those computed by inverse dynamics. This finding highlights a fundamental limitation of motion-only IL approaches, which may prioritize kinematics matching over physical consistency. Incorporating kinetic constraints, particularly ground reaction force and center of pressure information, significantly enhances the realism of internal and external kinetics. These findings suggest that, when imitation learning is applied to human-related research domains such as biomechanics and wearable robot co-design, kinetics-based reward shaping is necessary to achieve physically consistent gait representations.

</details>


### [176] [Predictive and adaptive maps for long-term visual navigation in changing environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12460)
*Lucie Halodova,Eliska Dvorakova,Filip Majer,Tomas Vintr,Oscar Martinez Mozos,Feras Dayoub,Tomas Krajnik*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不断变化的环境中进行长期视觉导航需要系统能够持续更新和优化其特征地图以适应外观变化，现有技术在这方面有待提高。

Method: 提出了几种地图管理策略，并评估了它们在长期教-学导航中的机器人定位精度。这些策略包括选择有用特征、移除过时特征和添加新特征。

Result: 实验结果表明，能够模拟环境外观的周期性变化并预测特定时间和地点可见特征的策略，优于那些没有明确模拟时间演变变化的策略。

Conclusion: 对于长期视觉导航，模拟环境外观的周期性变化和预测特征可见性是至关重要的，能够显著提高导航系统的鲁棒性和定位精度。

Abstract: In this paper, we compare different map management techniques for long-term visual navigation in changing environments. In this scenario, the navigation system needs to continuously update and refine its feature map in order to adapt to the environment appearance change. To achieve reliable long-term navigation, the map management techniques have to (i) select features useful for the current navigation task, (ii) remove features that are obsolete, (iii) and add new features from the current camera view to the map. We propose several map management strategies and evaluate their performance with regard to the robot localisation accuracy in long-term teach-and-repeat navigation. Our experiments, performed over three months, indicate that strategies which model cyclic changes of the environment appearance and predict which features are going to be visible at a particular time and location, outperform strategies which do not explicitly model the temporal evolution of the changes.

### [177] [Skill-informed Data-driven Haptic Nudges for High-dimensional Human Motor Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12583)
*Ankur Kamboj,Rajiv Ranganathan,Xiaobo Tan,Vaibhav Srivastava*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种数据驱动的、结合技能信息的框架，用于设计高维新颖运动学习任务中的最优触觉微调反馈。通过输入-输出隐马尔可夫模型（IOHMM）对人类运动学习的随机动力学进行建模，然后将触觉微调反馈设计问题形式化为部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），并从中推导出最优策略。人类受试者研究验证了该方法的有效性，表明与启发式反馈或无反馈相比，POMDP策略能够显著加速任务表现并促进学习者更快地发现高效的低维运动表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决高维新颖运动学习任务中，如何设计有效的触觉微调反馈以加速学习和提高表现的问题。

Method: 1. 使用输入-输出隐马尔可夫模型（IOHMM）对人类运动学习的随机动力学进行建模，区分潜在技能演化和可观察的运动学。2. 将触觉微调反馈设计问题形式化为部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）。3. 从POMDP推导出最优微调策略。

Result: 1. 与启发式反馈或无反馈组相比，POMDP策略训练的受试者任务表现显著加速。2. POMDP组的学习者更快地发现了高效的低维运动表示。

Conclusion: 提出的数据驱动的技能信息框架，通过POMDP推导的最优触觉微调策略，能够有效加速高维新颖运动学习任务的表现，并帮助学习者更快地掌握高效的运动控制策略。

Abstract: In this work, we propose a data-driven skill-informed framework to design optimal haptic nudge feedback for high-dimensional novel motor learning tasks. We first model the stochastic dynamics of human motor learning using an Input-Output Hidden Markov Model (IOHMM), which explicitly decouples latent skill evolution from observable kinematic emissions. Leveraging this predictive model, we formulate the haptic nudge feedback design problem as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP). This allows us to derive an optimal nudging policy that minimizes long-term performance cost, implicitly guiding the learner toward robust regions of the skill space. We validated our approach through a human-subject study ($N=30$) using a high-dimensional hand-exoskeleton task. Results demonstrate that participants trained with the POMDP-derived policy exhibited significantly accelerated task performance compared to groups receiving heuristic-based feedback or no feedback. Furthermore, synergy analysis revealed that the POMDP group discovered efficient low-dimensional motor representations more rapidly.

### [178] [One-Step Flow Policy: Self-Distillation for Fast Visuomotor Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12480)
*Shaolong Li,Lichao Sun,Yongchao Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为OFP（One-Step Flow Policy）的框架，实现了高保真、单步动作生成，解决了生成模型在机器人控制中推理延迟高的问题，并在模拟和真实机器人任务中取得了比多步模型更好的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成模型（如流和扩散模型）在机器人控制中需要连续、多模态的动作分布，但其迭代采样方式导致推理延迟高，影响了控制频率和时敏操作的性能。

Method: 提出OFP（One-Step Flow Policy）框架，采用从头开始的自蒸馏方法实现单步动作生成。OFP包含自一致性损失（保证时间间隔内的连贯传输）和自指导正则化（使预测更接近专家模式）。此外，还引入了利用时间动作相关性来最小化生成传输距离的暖启动机制。

Result: 在56个不同的模拟操纵任务中，单步OFP取得了最先进的性能，比100步的扩散和流模型性能更优，并将动作生成速度提升了100倍以上。在RoboTwin 2.0的$π_{0.5}$模型集成中，单步OFP也超越了原有的10步策略。

Conclusion: OFP是一个实用且可扩展的解决方案，能够实现高精度、低延迟的机器人控制，克服了现有生成模型在推理速度上的瓶颈。

Abstract: Generative flow and diffusion models provide the continuous, multimodal action distributions needed for high-precision robotic policies. However, their reliance on iterative sampling introduces severe inference latency, degrading control frequency and harming performance in time-sensitive manipulation. To address this problem, we propose the One-Step Flow Policy (OFP), a from-scratch self-distillation framework for high-fidelity, single-step action generation without a pre-trained teacher. OFP unifies a self-consistency loss to enforce coherent transport across time intervals, and a self-guided regularization to sharpen predictions toward high-density expert modes. In addition, a warm-start mechanism leverages temporal action correlations to minimize the generative transport distance. Evaluations across 56 diverse simulated manipulation tasks demonstrate that a one-step OFP achieves state-of-the-art results, outperforming 100-step diffusion and flow policies while accelerating action generation by over $100\times$. We further integrate OFP into the $π_{0.5}$ model on RoboTwin 2.0, where one-step OFP surpasses the original 10-step policy. These results establish OFP as a practical, scalable solution for highly accurate and low-latency robot control.

</details>


### [179] [Reinforcement Learning for Elliptical Cylinder Motion Control Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12807)
*Pawel Marczewski,Paulina Superczynska,Jakub Bernat,Szymon Szczesny*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文研究了在有限扭矩下椭圆圆柱体的运动控制问题，并提出使用强化学习解决。文章还实现了一个基于能量整形和LQR的两阶段控制器作为基线进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受限于输入扭矩的设备控制问题具有挑战性，例如无绳磁力设备在远距离操作时输入扭矩受限。因此，研究椭圆圆柱体在有限扭矩下的运动控制具有实际意义。

Method: 使用强化学习来解决椭圆圆柱体在有限输入扭矩下的控制问题。作为基线，实现了一个两阶段控制器：一个能量整形摆动控制器用于将系统状态推向目标平衡点附近，然后一个局部LQR控制器用于稳定在目标姿态。

Result: 强化学习方法是可行的，但对于质量增加或长宽比差异大的椭圆圆柱体，在向上稳定或旋转半圈等情况下，学习到的策略会遇到困难。

Abstract: The control of devices with limited input always bring attention to solve by research due to its difficulty and non-trival solution. For instance, the inverted pendulum is benchmarking problem in control theory and machine learning. In this work, we are focused on the elliptical cylinder and its motion under limited torque. The inspiration of the problem is from untethered magnetic devices, which due to distance have to operate with limited input torque. In this work, the main goal is to define the control problem of elliptic cylinder with limited input torque and solve it by Reinforcement Learning. As a classical baseline, we evaluate a two-stage controller composed of an energy-shaping swing-up law and a local Linear Quadratic Regulator (LQR) stabilizer around the target equilibrium. The swing-up controller increases the system's mechanical energy to drive the state toward a neighborhood of the desired equilibrium, a linearization of the nonlinear model yields an LQR that regulates the angle and angular-rate states to the target orientation with bounded input. This swing-up + LQR policy is a strong, interpretable reference for underactuated system and serves a point of comparison to the learned policy under identical limits and parameters. The solution shows that the learning is possible however, the different cases like stabilization in upward position or rotating of half turn are very difficult for increasing mass or ellipses with a strongly unequal perimeter ratio.

### [180] [COAD: Constant-Time Planning for Continuous Goal Manipulation with Compressed Library and Online Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12488)
*Adil Shiyas,Zhuoyun Zhong,Constantinos Chamzas*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为COAD的框架，用于在连续的目标参数化任务空间中实现常数时间内的运动规划，通过离散化任务空间、存储代表性根问题的压缩库，并在查询时快速适应现有解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决机器人重复执行运动规划任务时，由于目标位置变化但工作空间固定而带来的效率问题，现有方法在覆盖连续任务空间和存储效率上存在不足。

Method: 将连续的任务空间离散化为有限的任务覆盖区域，只为代表性的根问题规划并存储解决方案，其他问题通过轻量级的适应模块（如线性插值、动态运动原语、轨迹优化）从根解决方案快速适应得到。

Result: 在各种机器人和环境中，COAD实现了运动库的大幅压缩，同时保持了高成功率和亚毫秒级的查询时间，在效率和路径质量上优于基线方法。

Conclusion: COAD框架能够高效地处理连续目标参数化任务空间中的运动规划问题，提供快速的查询响应和高质量的运动规划，并且具有良好的可压缩性和泛化性。

Abstract: In many robotic manipulation tasks, the robot repeatedly solves motion-planning problems that differ mainly in the location of the goal object and its associated obstacle, while the surrounding workspace remains fixed. Prior works have shown that leveraging experience and offline computation can accelerate repeated planning queries, but they lack guarantees of covering the continuous task space and require storing large libraries of solutions. In this work, we present COAD, a framework that provides constant-time planning over a continuous goal-parameterized task space. COAD discretizes the continuous task space into finitely many Task Coverage Regions. Instead of planning and storing solutions for every region offline, it constructs a compressed library by only solving representative root problems. Other problems are handled through fast adaptation from these root solutions. At query time, the system retrieves a root motion in constant time and adapts it to the desired goal using lightweight adaptation modules such as linear interpolation, Dynamic Movement Primitives, or simple trajectory optimization. We evaluate the framework on various manipulators and environments in simulation and the real world, showing that COAD achieves substantial compression of the motion library while maintaining high success rates and sub-millisecond-level queries, outperforming baseline methods in both efficiency and path quality. The source code is available at https://github.com/elpis-lab/CoAd.

</details>


### [181] [Robots that redesign themselves through kinematic self-destruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12505)
*Chen Yu,Sam Kriegman*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 这项研究介绍了一种能够通过“自我毁灭”来主动参与自身设计的机器人。它通过识别并移除阻碍运动的冗余连接，从而优化自身形态以实现更有效的运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人设计都是预先设定的，研究者希望探索一种机器人能够自主适应环境并优化自身设计的机制。

Method: 机器人使用单一的自回归序列模型作为控制器，在模拟环境中学习何时以及如何通过“自我毁灭”（移除冗余链接）来简化身体形态，并据此调整控制策略。学习到的策略随后被迁移到真实机器人上。

Result: 该机器人成功地通过自我毁灭优化了形态，并在真实环境中实现了比随机移除链接或无法移除链接的对照组更有效的向前运动。该方法还能泛化到未知的运动学树结构。

Conclusion: “自我设计”机器人（通过不可逆的“运动自毁”）可能比预先设计的机器人更具优势，并且这种策略可以作为一种通用的适应性策略应用于多种机器人。

Abstract: Every robot built to date was predesigned by an external process, prior to deployment. Here we show a robot that actively participates in its own design during its lifetime. Starting from a randomly assembled body, and using only proprioceptive feedback, the robot dynamically ``sculpts'' itself into a new design through kinematic self-destruction: identifying redundant links within its body that inhibit its locomotion, and then thrashing those links against the surface until they break at the joint and fall off the body. It does so using a single autoregressive sequence model, a universal controller that learns in simulation when and how to simplify a robot's body through self-destruction and then adaptively controls the reduced morphology. The optimized policy successfully transfers to reality and generalizes to previously unseen kinematic trees, generating forward locomotion that is more effective than otherwise equivalent policies that randomly remove links or cannot remove any. This suggests that self-designing robots may be more successful than predesigned robots in some cases, and that kinematic self-destruction, though reductive and irreversible, could provide a general adaptive strategy for a wide range of robots.

</details>


### [182] [From Passive Monitoring to Active Defence: Resilient Control of Manipulators Under Cyberattacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13003)
*Gabriele Gualandi,Alessandro V. Papadopoulos*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对冗余机械臂的、基于主动防御的抵御虚假数据注入攻击（FDIA）的架构，通过结合被动监测和主动控制策略，有效减小了攻击引起的末端执行器偏差，同时在无攻击情况下保持了任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于残差的被动异常检测器（如卡方检验）难以检测到能够诱导显著末端执行器偏差但又不触发警报的隐蔽性FDIA。因此，研究冗余机械臂对这类攻击的鲁棒性并提出主动防御机制是必要的。

Method: 本文构建了一个包含反馈线性化机械臂、稳态卡尔曼滤波器和基于卡方检验的异常检测器的闭环模型。在此基础上，提出了一种主动控制层面的防御机制，该机制利用一个新颖的、基于驱动投影的、无测量状态预测器产生的异常分数，通过一个单调函数来衰减控制输入。

Result: 所提出的主动防御设计为标称驱动损失提供了概率保证，并保持了闭环稳定性。从攻击者角度来看，推导了一个凸QCQP来计算一步最优隐蔽攻击。仿真结果表明，该防御机制显著减小了攻击诱导的末端执行器偏差，同时在无攻击时保持了标称任务性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的主动防御架构能够有效地增强冗余机械臂在面对隐蔽性FDIA时的鲁棒性，通过结合被动监测和主动控制，实现了对攻击的有效抵御，并保证了系统在正常运行下的性能。

Abstract: Cyber-physical robotic systems are vulnerable to false data injection attacks (FDIAs), in which an adversary corrupts sensor signals while evading residual-based passive anomaly detectors such as the chi-squared test. Such stealthy attacks can induce substantial end-effector deviations without triggering alarms. This paper studies the resilience of redundant manipulators to stealthy FDIAs and advances the architecture from passive monitoring to active defence. We formulate a closed-loop model comprising a feedback-linearized manipulator, a steady-state Kalman filter, and a chi-squared-based anomaly detector. Building on this passive monitoring layer, we propose an active control-level defence that attenuates the control input through a monotone function of an anomaly score generated by a novel actuation-projected, measurement-free state predictor. The proposed design provides probabilistic guarantees on nominal actuation loss and preserves closed-loop stability. From the attacker perspective, we derive a convex QCQP for computing one-step optimal stealthy attacks. Simulations on a 6-DOF planar manipulator show that the proposed defence significantly reduces attack-induced end-effector deviation while preserving nominal task performance in the absence of attacks.

### [183] [Red-Teaming Vision-Language-Action Models via Quality Diversity Prompt Generation for Robust Robot Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12510)
*Siddharth Srikanth,Freddie Liang,Sophie Hsu,Varun Bhatt,Shihan Zhao,Henry Chen,Bryon Tjanaka,Minjune Hwang,Akanksha Saran,Daniel Seita,Aaquib Tabrez,Stefanos Nikolaidis*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLA模型对语言指令的措辞非常敏感，难以预测其失败场景。本研究旨在提高VLA模型在不同措辞下的鲁棒性，特别是找出导致失败的自然语言任务描述。

Method: Q-DIG方法结合了高质量多样性（QD）技术和视觉语言模型（VLM），通过红队测试（red-teaming）生成一系列多样化的对抗性指令，暴露VLA模型的弱点。通过在模拟基准和真实世界环境中进行评估。

Result: Q-DIG能够找到比基线方法更多样化、更有意义的失败模式。在Q-DIG生成的指令上进行微调可以提高VLA模型的任务成功率。用户研究表明Q-DIG生成的提示更自然、更像人类。真实世界评估结果与模拟一致，微调进一步提高了对未见指令的成功率。

Conclusion: Q-DIG是一种有前景的方法，能够识别VLA模型的脆弱性并提高其鲁棒性，通过生成多样化且自然的对抗性指令来促进VLA模型的改进。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have significant potential to enable general-purpose robotic systems for a range of vision-language tasks. However, the performance of VLA-based robots is highly sensitive to the precise wording of language instructions, and it remains difficult to predict when such robots will fail. To improve the robustness of VLAs to different wordings, we present Q-DIG (Quality Diversity for Diverse Instruction Generation), which performs red-teaming by scalably identifying diverse natural language task descriptions that induce failures while remaining task-relevant. Q-DIG integrates Quality Diversity (QD) techniques with Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to generate a broad spectrum of adversarial instructions that expose meaningful vulnerabilities in VLA behavior. Our results across multiple simulation benchmarks show that Q-DIG finds more diverse and meaningful failure modes compared to baseline methods, and that fine-tuning VLAs on the generated instructions improves task success rates. Furthermore, results from a user study highlight that Q-DIG generates prompts judged to be more natural and human-like than those from baselines. Finally, real-world evaluations of Q-DIG prompts show results consistent with simulation, and fine-tuning VLAs on the generated prompts further success rates on unseen instructions. Together, these findings suggest that Q-DIG is a promising approach for identifying vulnerabilities and improving the robustness of VLA-based robots. Our anonymous project website is at qdigvla.github.io.

### [184] [Beyond Dense Futures: World Models as Structured Planners for Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12553)
*Minghao Jin,Mozheng Liao,Mingfei Han,Zhihui Li,Xiaojun Chang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出StructVLA，一种结合显式结构化规划和生成式世界模型的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）方法，用于改进机器人操作。该方法通过预测物理上有意义的稀疏结构化帧，而不是密集预测或高层语义目标，来解决现有方法的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于世界模型的VLA架构在预测未来时存在视觉冗余和误差累积问题，导致长期规划漂移。而稀疏方法缺乏明确的运动学约束，难以与低层执行对齐。因此，需要一种能够进行可靠控制并弥合规划与执行之间差距的方法。

Method: StructVLA将生成式世界模型重构为显式结构化规划器。它不进行密集预测或预测语义目标，而是预测稀疏、物理上有意义的结构化帧。这些帧通过抓手过渡和运动学转折点等内在运动学线索导出，与任务进展紧密对齐。该方法采用两阶段训练范式，先训练世界模型预测结构化帧，然后优化模型将结构化预测映射到低层动作。

Result: StructVLA在SimplerEnv-WidowX上实现了75.0%的平均成功率，在LIBERO上达到了94.8%的成功率。实际部署也证明了其在基本抓取和放置以及复杂的长期任务上的可靠性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: StructVLA通过预测稀疏的、具有物理意义的结构化帧，有效地解决了现有VLA方法在长期规划和低层执行对齐方面的挑战，为机器人控制提供了清晰的物理指导，并在模拟和真实世界环境中均取得了优异的性能。

Abstract: Recent world-model-based Vision-Language-Action (VLA) architectures have improved robotic manipulation through predictive visual foresight. However, dense future prediction introduces visual redundancy and accumulates errors, causing long-horizon plan drift. Meanwhile, recent sparse methods typically represent visual foresight using high-level semantic subtasks or implicit latent states. These representations often lack explicit kinematic grounding, weakening the alignment between planning and low-level execution. To address this, we propose StructVLA, which reformulates a generative world model into an explicit structured planner for reliable control. Instead of dense rollouts or semantic goals, StructVLA predicts sparse, physically meaningful structured frames. Derived from intrinsic kinematic cues (e.g., gripper transitions and kinematic turning points), these frames capture spatiotemporal milestones closely aligned with task progress. We implement this approach through a two-stage training paradigm with a unified discrete token vocabulary: the world model is first trained to predict structured frames and subsequently optimized to map the structured foresight into low-level actions. This approach provides clear physical guidance and bridges visual planning and motion control. In our experiments, StructVLA achieves strong average success rates of 75.0% on SimplerEnv-WidowX and 94.8% on LIBERO. Real-world deployments further demonstrate reliable task completion and robust generalization across both basic pick-and-place and complex long-horizon tasks.

### [186] [CarPLAN: Context-Adaptive and Robust Planning with Dynamic Scene Awareness for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12607)
*Junyong Yun,Jungho Kim,ByungHyun Lee,Dongyoung Lee,Sehwan Choi,Seunghyeop Nam,Kichun Jo,Jun Won Choi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为CarPLAN的模仿学习（IL）框架，用于解决自动驾驶中的运动规划问题。CarPLAN通过引入位移感知预测编码（DPE）来增强模型对空间关系的理解，并通过上下文自适应多专家解码器（CMD）来处理多样的驾驶场景，实现了在复杂交通场景下的自适应规划，并在nuPlan和Waymax基准测试中取得了最先进的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于IL的运动规划方法在处理真实世界驾驶数据时，往往难以充分捕捉复杂的驾驶上下文信息，并进行上下文自适应决策，这限制了其在安全可靠的实际应用。因此，研究需要能够增强驾驶上下文理解并适应不同交通场景的IL运动规划框架。

Method: 本文提出CarPLAN框架，包含两个主要创新点：1. 位移感知预测编码（DPE）：预测自驾车（AV）与周围场景元素之间的未来位移向量，以提升模型的空间感知能力，并考虑相对距离进行轨迹生成。2. 上下文自适应多专家解码器（CMD）：利用专家混合（MoE）框架，在每个Transformer层动态选择最适合的专家解码器，以适应不同的驾驶上下文。

Result: CarPLAN在nuPlan基准测试中表现出最先进的性能，在所有闭环模拟指标上均优于现有方法。在Test14-Hard等具有挑战性的场景下，CarPLAN展现出鲁棒的性能。在Waymax基准测试上的额外实验进一步证明了其跨不同基准设置的泛化能力。

Conclusion: CarPLAN通过显式地增强驾驶上下文理解和实现跨不同驾驶场景的自适应规划，有效地解决了模仿学习在自动驾驶运动规划中的局限性，并在基准测试中取得了优异且鲁棒的性能，验证了其在复杂驾驶条件下的有效性。

Abstract: Imitation learning (IL) is widely used for motion planning in autonomous driving due to its data efficiency and access to real-world driving data. For safe and robust real-world driving, IL-based planning requires capturing the complex driving contexts inherent in real-world data and enabling context-adaptive decision-making, rather than relying solely on expert trajectory imitation. In this paper, we propose CarPLAN, a novel IL-based motion planning framework that explicitly enhances driving context understanding and enables adaptive planning across diverse traffic scenarios. Our contributions are twofold: We introduce Displacement-Aware Predictive Encoding (DPE) to improve the model's spatial awareness by predicting future displacement vectors between the Autonomous Vehicle (AV) and surrounding scene elements. This allows the planner to account for relational spacing when generating trajectories. In addition to the standard imitation loss, we incorporate an augmented loss term that captures displacement prediction errors, ensuring planning decisions consider relative distances from other agents. To improve the model's ability to handle diverse driving contexts, we propose Context-Adaptive Multi-Expert Decoder (CMD), which leverages the Mixture of Experts (MoE) framework. CMD dynamically selects the most suitable expert decoders based on scene structure at each Transformer layer, enabling adaptive and context-aware planning in dynamic environments. We evaluate CarPLAN on the nuPlan benchmark and demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across all closed-loop simulation metrics. In particular, CarPLAN exhibits robust performance on challenging scenarios such as Test14-Hard, validating its effectiveness in complex driving conditions. Additional experiments on the Waymax benchmark further demonstrate its generalization capability across different benchmark settings.

This paper presents a framework for autonomous integration and continuous improvement of robotic assembly systems based on Skill Graph representations. A Skill Graph organizes robot capabilities as verb-based skills, explicitly linking semantic descriptions (verbs and nouns) with executable policies, pre-conditions, post-conditions, and evaluators. We show how Skill Graphs enable rapid system integration by supporting semantic-level planning over skills, while simultaneously grounding execution through well-defined interfaces to robot controllers and perception modules. After initial deployment, the same Skill Graph structure supports systematic data collection and closed-loop performance improvement, enabling iterative refinement of skills and their composition. We demonstrate how this approach unifies system configuration, execution, evaluation, and learning within a single representation, providing a scalable pathway toward adaptive and reusable robotic assembly systems. The code is at https://github.com/intelligent-control-lab/AIDF.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLA模型在涉及视觉遮挡、精细操作和物理接触的任务中表现不佳，因为它们主要依赖视觉和语言信息。

Method: 通过将触觉模态整合到基于Transformer的策略中，并引入一个接触感知门控机制，该机制仅在检测到接触时激活触觉Token，实现自适应多模态融合，并利用Transformer架构处理融合后的视觉、语言和触觉Token。

Result: 在约束锁定拆卸、箱内拾取和鲁棒性评估等任务中，TacVLA模型相比基线模型取得了更好的性能，平均成功率在拆卸任务中提高了20%，在箱内拾取任务中提高了60%，在视觉遮挡场景下提高了2.1倍。

Conclusion: TacVLA通过整合触觉模态，能够有效地增强VLA模型在接触丰富交互中的精细操作能力，特别是在视觉遮挡和物理接触等具有挑战性的场景下，显著提高了机器人的任务完成性能。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have demonstrated significant advantages in robotic manipulation. However, their reliance on vision and language often leads to suboptimal performance in tasks involving visual occlusion, fine-grained manipulation, and physical contact. To address these challenges, we propose TacVLA, a fine-tuned VLA model by incorporating tactile modalities into the transformer-based policy to enhance fine-grained manipulation capabilities. Specifically, we introduce a contact-aware gating mechanism that selectively activates tactile tokens only when contact is detected, enabling adaptive multimodal fusion while avoiding irrelevant tactile interference. The fused visual, language, and tactile tokens are jointly processed within the transformer architecture to strengthen cross-modal grounding during contact-rich interaction. Extensive experiments on constraint-locked disassembly, in-box picking and robustness evaluations demonstrate that our model outperforms baselines, improving the performance by averaging 20% success rate in disassembly, 60% in in-box picking and 2.1x improvement in scenarios with visual occlusion. Videos are available at https://sites.google.com/view/tacvla and code will be released.

In this work, we propose LATENT, a system that Learns Athletic humanoid TEnnis skills from imperfect human motioN daTa. The imperfect human motion data consist only of motion fragments that capture the primitive skills used when playing tennis rather than precise and complete human-tennis motion sequences from real-world tennis matches, thereby significantly reducing the difficulty of data collection. Our key insight is that, despite being imperfect, such quasi-realistic data still provide priors about human primitive skills in tennis scenarios. With further correction and composition, we learn a humanoid policy that can consistently strike incoming balls under a wide range of conditions and return them to target locations, while preserving natural motion styles. We also propose a series of designs for robust sim-to-real transfer and deploy our policy on the Unitree G1 humanoid robot. ### [190] [HaltNav: Reactive Visual Halting over Lightweight Topological Priors for Robust Vision-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12696)
*Pingcong Li,Zihui Yu,Bichi Zhang,Sören Schwertfeger*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 HaltNav 的分层导航框架，用于在视觉语言导航（VLN）任务中实现开放词汇、面向目标的自主性。它结合了轻量级的文本地图（osmAG）进行全局规划和基于多模态大型语言模型（MLLM）的大脑模块进行局部探索和障碍处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的 VLN 研究正从遵循固定指令转向更灵活的开放词汇自主导航。现有的方法依赖于计算成本高的 2D/3D 地图，或者在局部导航时容易因环境变化（如门关闭）而失败。研究动机是开发一种更鲁棒、更轻量级的导航方法，能够处理真实世界中动态变化的环境。

Method: HaltNav 采用分层方法：1. 全局规划：利用 osmAG（基于 OpenStreetMap 的拓扑地图）进行全局路径规划。2. 大脑模块：一个 MLLM 模块将全局路线转换为局部执行片段，并具备障碍物感知能力。3. 局部执行与障碍处理：VLN 执行器根据子指令进行导航，并通过 Reactive Visual Halting (RVH) 机制检测局部障碍。RVH 会中断局部控制，更新 osmAG，并触发重新规划。4. 数据合成：使用生成模型合成包含真实障碍物的训练数据，以增强模型对困难负样本的鲁棒性。

Result: HaltNav 在没有冗长语言指令的情况下，在多种 VLN 任务中超越了现有基线方法。在面对环境变化（如障碍物）时，其鲁棒性显著提高，尤其是在长距离导航任务中。

Conclusion: HaltNav 通过结合轻量级拓扑地图的全局规划能力和 MLLM 的局部理解与反应能力，有效地解决了真实世界 VLN 中环境变化的挑战。该框架提高了导航的鲁棒性和自主性，是迈向更通用 VLN 系统的有效途径。

Abstract: Vision-and-Language Navigation (VLN) is shifting from rigid, step-by-step instruction following toward open-vocabulary, goal-oriented autonomy. Achieving this transition without exhaustive routing prompts requires agents to leverage structural priors. While prior work often assumes computationally heavy 2D/3D metric maps, we instead exploit a lightweight, text-based osmAG (OpenStreetMap Area Graph), a floorplan-level topological representation that is easy to obtain and maintain. However, global planning over a prior map alone is brittle in real-world deployments, where local connectivity can change (e.g., closed doors or crowded passages), leading to execution-time failures. To address this gap, we propose a hierarchical navigation framework HaltNav that couples the robust global planning of osmAG with the local exploration and instruction-grounding capability of VLN. Our approach features an MLLM-based brain module, which is capable of high-level task grounding and obstruction awareness. Conditioned on osmAG, the brain converts the global route into a sequence of localized execution snippets, providing the VLN executor with prior-grounded, goal-centric sub-instructions. Meanwhile, it detects local anomalies via a mechanism we term Reactive Visual Halting (RVH), which interrupts the local control loop, updates osmAG by invalidating the corresponding topology, and triggers replanning to orchestrate a viable detour. To train this halting capability efficiently, we introduce a data synthesis pipeline that leverages generative models to inject realistic obstacles into otherwise navigable scenes, substantially enriching hard negative samples. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our hierarchical framework outperforms several baseline methods without tedious language instructions, and significantly improves robustness for long-horizon vision-language navigation under environmental changes.

Abstract: Panoramic imagery provides holistic 360° visual coverage for perception in quadruped robots. However, existing occupancy prediction methods are mainly designed for wheeled autonomous driving and rely heavily on RGB cues, limiting their robustness in complex environments. To bridge this gap, (1) we present PanoMMOcc, the first real-world panoramic multimodal occupancy dataset for quadruped robots, featuring four sensing modalities across diverse scenes. (2) We propose a panoramic multimodal occupancy perception framework, VoxelHound, tailored for legged mobility and spherical imaging. Specifically, we design (i) a Vertical Jitter Compensation (VJC) module to mitigate severe viewpoint perturbations caused by body pitch and roll during mobility, enabling more consistent spatial reasoning, and (ii) an effective Multimodal Information Prompt Fusion (MIPF) module that jointly leverages panoramic visual cues and auxiliary modalities to enhance volumetric occupancy prediction. (3) We establish a benchmark based on PanoMMOcc and provide detailed data analysis to enable systematic evaluation of perception methods under challenging embodied scenarios. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VoxelHound achieves state-of-the-art performance on PanoMMOcc (+4.16%} in mIoU). The dataset and code will be publicly released to facilitate future research on panoramic multimodal 3D perception for embodied robotic systems at https://github.com/SXDR/PanoMMOcc, along with the calibration tools released at https://github.com/losehu/CameraLiDAR-Calib.

### [192] [Altered Thoughts, Altered Actions: Probing Chain-of-Thought Vulnerabilities in VLA Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12717)
*Tuan Duong Trinh,Naveed Akhtar,Basim Azam*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 研究表明，机器人视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在执行任务时，其内部推理文本中的实体指代（例如物体名称）的完整性比推理的逻辑性或顺序结构更重要。攻击者可以通过替换推理文本中的物体名称来显著降低机器人的任务成功率，而对输入进行修改或生成看似合理的错误推理则影响甚微。这种漏洞仅存在于使用链式思考（CoT）的VLA模型中，表明内部推理文本是一个新的、隐蔽的攻击向量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型越来越多地采用链式思考（CoT）进行推理，在生成动作指令前会产生一段自然语言计划。研究人员想知道，动作解码器究竟依赖于这个中间文本计划的哪些特性，并且仅通过破坏推理过程（而不改变输入）是否会影响机器人的实际任务表现。

Method: 研究人员设计了一个包含七种文本破坏方式的分类体系，分为三个攻击者层级（盲噪声、机械-语义、LLM自适应）。他们将这些攻击应用于一个先进的推理VLA模型，并在40个LIBERO桌面操作任务上进行了测试。此外，还通过一个非推理VLA模型进行了交叉架构控制实验，以验证漏洞的独特性。

Result: 结果显示，替换推理文本中的物体名称会将整体成功率降低8.3个百分点，在目标条件任务上降至-19.3个百分点，在单个任务上更是高达-45个百分点。而句子重排、空间方向反转、标记噪声，甚至由一个700亿参数的LLM生成的看似合理但错误的计划，其影响都在±4个百分点以内。这表明动作解码器更依赖于实体指代的完整性，而非推理质量或顺序结构。特别是，一个复杂的基于LLM的攻击者表现不如简单的机械式物体名称替换，因为保留了合理性反而无意中保留了解码器所需的实体关联结构。非推理VLA模型的交叉架构控制证实了该漏洞仅存在于增强推理的模型中。

Conclusion: 动作解码器对VLA模型内部推理文本中的实体指代（如物体名称）的完整性高度敏感，对推理质量和顺序结构的依赖性较低。仅通过修改推理文本中的物体名称就能显著降低机器人的任务成功率，这揭示了一个新的、不易察觉的攻击向量，对现有基于输入的防御机制具有隐蔽性。

Abstract: Recent Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models increasingly adopt chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning, generating a natural-language plan before decoding motor commands. This internal text channel between the reasoning module and the action decoder has received no adversarial scrutiny. We ask: which properties of this intermediate plan does the action decoder actually rely on, and can targeted corruption of the reasoning trace alone -- with all inputs left intact -- degrade a robot's physical task performance? We design a taxonomy of seven text corruptions organized into three attacker tiers (blind noise, mechanical-semantic, and LLM-adaptive) and apply them to a state-of-the-art reasoning VLA across 40 LIBERO tabletop manipulation tasks. Our results reveal a striking asymmetry: substituting object names in the reasoning trace reduces overall success rate by 8.3~percentage points (pp) -- reaching $-$19.3~pp on goal-conditioned tasks and $-$45~pp on individual tasks -- whereas sentence reordering, spatial-direction reversal, token noise, and even a 70B-parameter LLM crafting plausible-but-wrong plans all have negligible impact (within $\pm$4~pp). This asymmetry indicates that the action decoder depends on entity-reference integrity rather than reasoning quality or sequential structure. Notably, a sophisticated LLM-based attacker underperforms simple mechanical object-name substitution, because preserving plausibility inadvertently retains the entity-grounding structure the decoder needs. A cross-architecture control using a non-reasoning VLA confirms the vulnerability is exclusive to reasoning-augmented models, while instruction-level attacks degrade both architectures -- establishing that the internal reasoning trace is a distinct and stealthy threat vector invisible to input-validation defenses.

</details>


### [193] [AnchorVLA4D: an Anchor-Based Spatial-Temporal Vision-Language-Action Model for Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12730)
*Juan Zhu,Zhanying Shao,Xiaoqi Li,Ethan Morgan,Jiadong Xu,Hongwei Fan,Hao Dong*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出AnchorVLA4D，一种增强视觉-语言-动作（VLA）系统在机器人操作中空间和时间推理能力的模型，通过引入视觉锚点和轻量级空间编码器，无需额外传感器即可显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLA系统在空间感知和记忆方面存在局限，导致在操作过程中容易遗忘物体和迷失方向。

Method: 提出AnchorVLA4D，通过引入一个“锚点图像”来保留初始场景上下文，并采用轻量级空间编码器联合处理锚点和当前帧，以揭示几何关系。模型基于Qwen2.5-VL骨干网络，动作头部采用基于扩散的模型，且无需额外传感器。

Result: AnchorVLA4D在Simpler WidowX基准上实现了13.6%的性能提升，并在真实世界任务中取得了80%的平均成功率。

Conclusion: 视觉锚点和轻量级空间编码器是增强VLA系统在机器人操作中空间和时间推理能力的有效方法，AnchorVLA4D在仿真和真实世界中均表现出优越的性能。

Abstract: Since current Vision-Language-Action (VLA) systems suffer from limited spatial perception and the absence of memory throughout manipulation, we investigate visual anchors as a means to enhance spatial and temporal reasoning within VLA policies for robotic manipulation. Conventional VLAs generate actions by conditioning on a single current frame together with a language instruction. However, since the frame is encoded as a 2D image, it does not contain detailed spatial information, and the VLA similarly lacks any means to incorporate past context. As a result, it frequently forgets objects under occlusion and becomes spatially disoriented during the manipulation process. Thus, we propose AnchorVLA4D, a simple spatial-temporal VLA that augments the visual input with an anchor image to preserve the initial scene context throughout execution, and adds a lightweight spatial encoder that jointly processes the anchor and current frames to expose geometric relationships within an episode. Built on a Qwen2.5-VL backbone with a diffusion-based action head, AnchorVLA4D requires no additional sensing modalities (e.g., depth or point clouds) and introduces negligible inference overhead. Combining anchoring with a frozen pretrained spatial encoder yields further gains, realizing a 13.6% improvement on the Simpler WidowX benchmark and confirming the approach on real-world tasks, where it achieved an average success rate of 80%.

Method: 提出了一种名为Flow-Aware Multi-Agent Path Finding (FA-MAPF)的框架，该框架将学习到的不可控代理的运动模式集成到中心化的MAPF算法中。

Abstract: Deploying multi-robot systems in environments shared with dynamic and uncontrollable agents presents significant challenges, especially for large robot fleets. While existing research primarily focuses on preserving the completeness of Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) solutions considering delays, there is limited emphasis on utilizing additional environmental information to enhance solution quality in the presence of other dynamic agents. To this end, we propose Flow-Aware Multi-Agent Path Finding (FA-MAPF), a novel framework that integrates learned motion patterns of uncontrollable agents into centralized MAPF algorithms. Our evaluation, conducted on a diverse set of benchmark maps with simulated uncontrollable agents and on a real-world map with recorded human trajectories, demonstrates the effectiveness of FA-MAPF compared to state-of-the-art baselines. The experimental results show that FA-MAPF can consistently reduce conflicts with uncontrollable agents, up to 55%, without compromising task efficiency.

### [195] [Easy-IIL: Reducing Human Operational Burden in Interactive Imitation Learning via Assistant Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12769)
*Chengjie Zhang,Chao Tang,Wenlong Dong,Dehao Huang,Aoxiang Gu,Hong Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 Easy-IIL 的交互式模仿学习框架，该框架利用预训练的模型学习方法作为辅助专家来收集大部分数据，人类专家只需提供一次演示和在关键时刻进行干预，从而显著减轻了人类操作负担，同时保持了与主流 IIL 方法相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的交互式模仿学习（IIL）方法需要大量的人类参与，无论是离线演示还是在线互动。本文关注的是减少人类在数据收集过程中的主动操作负担，并借鉴了模型学习方法在数据稀疏情况下表现优于端到端方法但数据量增加后性能落后的观察，旨在结合两者的优势。

Method: Easy-IIL 框架使用现成的模型学习方法作为“助手专家”。人类专家仅提供一个初始演示，然后助手专家负责大部分的数据收集。当助手专家的行为接近失败时，人类专家才会介入进行纠正。Easy-IIL 还通过保留离线和在线数据的质量来维持 IIL 的性能。

Result: 在仿真和真实世界实验中，Easy-IIL 显著降低了人类专家的操作负担，并且性能与主流 IIL 基线相当。用户研究也证实了 Easy-IIL 降低了人类专家的主观工作量。

Conclusion: Easy-IIL 框架成功地利用模型学习方法来减少交互式模仿学习中的人类操作需求，同时保持了学习性能，并在用户研究中得到了验证。

Abstract: Interactive Imitation Learning (IIL) typically relies on extensive human involvement for both offline demonstration and online interaction. Prior work primarily focuses on reducing human effort in passive monitoring rather than active operation. Interestingly, structured model-based imitation approaches achieve comparable performance with significantly fewer demonstrations than end-to-end imitation learning policies in the low-data regime. However, these methods are typically surpassed by end-to-end policies as the data increases. Leveraging this insight, we propose Easy-IIL, a framework that utilizes off-the-shelf model-based imitation methods as an assistant expert to replace active human operation for the majority of data collection. The human expert only provides a single demonstration to initialize the assistant expert and intervenes in critical states where the task is approaching failure. Furthermore, Easy-IIL can maintain IIL performance by preserving both offline and online data quality. Extensive simulation and real-world experiments demonstrate that Easy-IIL significantly reduces human operational burden while maintaining performance comparable to mainstream IIL baselines. User studies further confirm that Easy-IIL reduces subjective workload on the human expert. Project page: https://sites.google.com/view/easy-iil

</details>

Abstract: Quadrotor endurance is ultimately limited by battery behavior, yet most energy aware planning treats the battery as a simple energy reservoir and overlooks how flight motions induce dynamic current loads that accelerate battery degradation. This work presents an end to end framework for motion aware battery health assessment in quadrotors. We first design a wide range current sensing module to capture motion specific current profiles during real flights, preserving transient features. In parallel, a high fidelity battery model is calibrated using reference performance tests and a metaheuristic based on a degradation coupled electrochemical model.By simulating measured flight loads in the calibrated model, we systematically resolve how different flight motions translate into degradation modes loss of lithium inventory and loss of active material as well as internal side reactions. The results demonstrate that even when two flight profiles consume the same average energy, their transient load structures can drive different degradation pathways, emphasizing the need for motion-aware battery management that balances efficiency with battery degradation.

### [197] [FLUX: Accelerating Cross-Embodiment Generative Navigation Policies via Rectified Flow and Static-to-Dynamic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12806)
*Zeying Gong,Yangyi Zhong,Yiyi Ding,Tianshuai Hu,Guoyang Zhao,Lingdong Kong,Rong Li,Jiadi You,Junwei Liang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出 DynBench：一个包含物理有效人群模拟的动态导航基准，并结合现有静态协议，覆盖六种基本导航任务。2. 提出 FLUX：一种基于流模型的统一导航策略，通过线性化概率流将迭代去噪替换为直线轨迹，提高了推理效率。3. 采用静态到动态的课程学习方法，先在静态环境下学习几何先验，再通过强化学习在动态社交环境中进行优化。

Result: FLUX 在所有导航任务上均取得了最先进的性能。与先前基于流的模型相比，FLUX 的每步推理效率提高了 47%，与基于扩散的模型相比提高了 29%。FLUX 还展示了零样本的跨平台（轮式、四足、人形机器人）模拟到现实迁移能力，无需进行任何微调。

Conclusion: DynBench 是一个强大的动态导航评估框架，FLUX 作为首个基于流的统一导航策略，在效率和性能上均取得了显著突破，并展现了出色的通用性和迁移能力，为未来的自动导航研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Autonomous navigation requires a broad spectrum of skills, from static goal-reaching to dynamic social traversal, yet evaluation remains fragmented across disparate protocols. We introduce DynBench, a dynamic navigation benchmark featuring physically valid crowd simulation. Combined with existing static protocols, it supports comprehensive evaluation across six fundamental navigation tasks. Within this framework, we propose FLUX, the first flow-based unified navigation policy. By linearizing probability flow, FLUX replaces iterative denoising with straight-line trajectories, improving per-step inference efficiency by 47% over prior flow-based methods and 29% over diffusion-based ones. Following a static-to-dynamic curriculum, FLUX initially establishes geometric priors and is subsequently refined through reinforcement learning in dynamic social environments. This regime not only strengthens socially-aware navigation but also enhances static task robustness by capturing recovery behaviors through stochastic action distributions. FLUX achieves state-of-the-art performance across all tasks and demonstrates zero-shot sim-to-real transfer on wheeled, quadrupedal, and humanoid platforms without any fine-tuning.

### [198] [SmoothTurn: Learning to Turn Smoothly for Agile Navigation with Quadrupedal Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12842)
*Zunzhi You,Haolan Guo,Yunke Wang,Chang Xu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为SmoothTurn的学习框架，用于实现四足机器人在高速奔跑中进行敏捷的连续转向，以解决现有方法在连续目标切换时动量损失的问题。该框架通过引入序列化目标达成奖励、包含未来目标信息的观测空间以及自动目标课程，有效地提升了机器人的转向平滑度和整体机动性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有四足机器人敏捷导航方法通常是单目标导向，在需要连续转向时，无法保持动量并预测未来动作，限制了机器人的机动潜力。因此，研究能够进行平滑连续转向的敏捷导航方法具有重要意义。

Method: 本文将连续目标导航任务形式化为序列化局部导航，并引入了SmoothTurn学习框架。该框架包含三个关键创新：1. 序列化目标达成奖励，鼓励机器人在连续目标切换时保持动量；2. 扩展的观测空间，加入未来目标信息（lookahead window）；3. 自动目标课程（automatic goal curriculum），逐步增加目标序列的难度。训练好的策略可直接部署于真实机器人。

Result: 实验结果表明，SmoothTurn框架能够学习到敏捷的运动策略，实现平滑的连续转向。涌现出的行为包括：在目标切换时控制动量、提前面向未来目标以及规划高效路径。仿真和真实机器人实验均验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: SmoothTurn框架成功实现了四足机器人在高速奔跑中的敏捷序列化局部导航，显著提升了转向的平滑度和机动性，克服了传统单目标方法的局限性，并展现出对动量控制、前瞻性转向和路径规划等高级行为的自主学习能力。

Abstract: Quadrupedal robots show great potential for valuable real-world applications such as fire rescue and industrial inspection. Such applications often require urgency and the ability to navigate agilely, which in turn demands the capability to change directions smoothly while running in high speed. Existing approaches for agile navigation typically learn a single-goal reaching policy by encouraging the robot to stay at the target position after reaching there. As a result, when the policy is used to reach sequential goals that require changing directions, it cannot anticipate upcoming maneuvers or maintain momentum across the switch of goals, thereby preventing the robot from fully exploiting its agility potential. In this work, we formulate the task as sequential local navigation, extending the single-goal-conditioned local navigation formulation in prior work. We then introduce SmoothTurn, a learning-based control framework that learns to turn smoothly while running rapidly for agile sequential local navigation. The framework adopts a novel sequential goal-reaching reward, an expanded observation space with a lookahead window for future goals, and an automatic goal curriculum that progressively expands the difficulty of sampled goal sequences based on the goal-reaching performance. The trained policy can be directly deployed on real quadrupedal robots with onboard sensors and computation. Both simulation and real-world empirical results show that SmoothTurn learns an agile locomotion policy that performs smooth turning across goals, with emergent behaviors such as controlling momentum when switching goals, facing towards the future goal in advance, and planning efficient paths. We have provided video demos of the learned motions in the supplementary materials. The source code and trained policies will be made available upon acceptance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Diffusion-based robot navigation policies trained on large-scale imitation learning datasets, can generate multi-modal trajectories directly from the robot's visual observations, bypassing the traditional localization-mapping-planning pipeline and achieving strong zero-shot generalization. However, their performance remains constrained by the coverage of offline datasets, and when deployed in unseen settings, distribution shift often leads to accumulated trajectory errors and safety-critical failures. Adapting diffusion policies with reinforcement learning is challenging because their iterative denoising structure hinders effective gradient backpropagation, while also making the training of an additional value network computationally expensive and less stable. To address these issues, we propose a reinforcement learning fine-tuning framework tailored for diffusion-based navigation. The method leverages the inherent multi-trajectory sampling mechanism of diffusion models and adopts Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), which estimates relative advantages across sampled trajectories without requiring a separate value network. To preserve pretrained representations while enabling adaptation, we freeze the visual encoder and selectively update the higher decoder layers and action head, enhancing safety-aware behaviors through online environmental feedback. On the PointGoal task in Isaac Sim, our approach improves the Success Rate from 52.0% to 58.7% and SPL from 0.49 to 0.54 on unseen scenes, while reducing collision frequency. Additional experiments show that the fine-tuned policy transfers zero-shot to a real quadruped platform and maintains stable performance in geometrically out-of-distribution environments, suggesting improved adaptability and safe generalization to new domains.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在一个高效的多状态约束卡尔曼滤波器（MSCKF）框架内，利用滑动窗口中的平面特征构建共面约束，并通过零空间投影消除对特征参数的依赖。引入并行体素数据关联和紧凑的聚类到平面测量模型，以提高效率并加速更新过程。
